Commented by dgroz093@xxx on 02Â Jan 2011

Look, obviously a quad break vivisect isn’t an easy thing to survive. There’s a reason it takes like 6 minutes to set up. The thing to exploit here is parry.

My strategy was always to keep my parry on my legs until I thought I was getting close to breaking, then flick it over to my arms. If he double breaks your legs with benzene, heal one and shield while puffing on rebounding. If he tries to break your arms, you’ll parry one and he’s back to square 0.

The real danger is that he’ll double break your legs with opium for the prone. If he breaks them with something else though, you’re in with a chance.

Of course, in this case Vierra doesn’t seem to have parried anything…
